[30;1m129 | [0m[35m```pydruid.async_client.AsyncPyDruid``` implements an asynchronous client. To achieve that, it utili[0m
[30;1m130 | [0m[35mHTTP client from ```Tornado``` framework. The asynchronous client is suitable for use with async fra[0m
[30;1m131 | [0m[35mand provides much better performance at scale. It lets you serve multiple requests at the same time,[0m
